FNV PBR PPLIGHTING PASS SHADER PAIR CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which functions read PPLighting global shader arrays after creation?
2. How are vertex groups 0x011FDD88/0x011FDE04/0x011FDE5C paired with pixel groups 0x011FDA48/0x011FDB08?
3. Which pair is written into current pass +0x5C/+0x44 before SetShaders?
4. Is there one safe PPLighting family for first visible side-table replacement?

Compatibility rule:
Do not bind a replacement PBR shader until the array-to-pass pair and input family are proven.
